┃ Note on Period of Performance discrepancy: Page 3 lists 09/08/2025–09/07/2026; Page 9 lists Base 09/01/2025–08/31/2026 with options [RFP pp. 3, 9]. We will reconcile at award and         ┃
┃ baseline the IMS within 10 business days.                                                                                                                                                  ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  3 Technical Approach 3.1 ETL (Informatica PowerCenter) [RFP pp. 13, 24]                                                                                                                   ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • Governed ingestion from authoritative sources; parameterized mappings; DQ rules and scorecards; lineage and metadata; pushdown optimization/tuning to Oracle.                           ┃
┃  • Scheduling/monitoring with restartability; logs to SIEM; mask test data for non-prod.                                                                                                   ┃
┃  • Targets: ≥99.5% job success; nightly load latency <60 minutes; priority event streams <5 minutes.                                                                                       ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃ 3.2 System Administration [RFP pp. 14, 25, 90]                                                                                                                                             ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • Patch baselines (CIS/STIG), backup/restore, HA/DR runbooks, capacity planning; operations on Government networks with GFE only.                                                         ┃
┃  • FIPS 140-2-validated encryption, TLS 1.2+; configuration drift <2%; documented CAB process.                                                                                             ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃ 3.3 Database Administration (Oracle) [RFP pp. 14, 25; standards p. 9, 36]                                                                                                                  ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • Oracle on AWS (RDS/EC2) with Multi-AZ/Data Guard; TDE and TLS; AWR-driven tuning; PITR; back-up lifecycle to meet RTO 4h / RPO 15m.                                                     ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃ 3.4 API Development (Java 8/Spring Boot) & Integration [RFP pp. 15, 26, 29]                                                                                                                ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • API design/governance; OpenAPI; authN/Z with SAML/OIDC; PIV/mTLS where required.                                                                                                        ┃
┃  • Testing pyramid + load tests; logging/observability; versioning and deprecation policy.                                                                                                 ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃ 3.5 Geospatial Services [RFP pp. 3, 29]                                                                                                                                                    ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃

┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • ATO artifacts (SSP, SAR, POA&M, ConMon) per NIST SP 800-53 Mod; DHS 4300A tailoring and overlays; evidence automation and monthly updates [RFP pp. 39–41, 58, 98].                      ┃
┃  • FIPS 140-2 encryption for data-in-transit/at-rest; CUI protection; email encryption for CUI [RFP pp. 37, 41, 76, 78].                                                                   ┃
┃  • ICAM/MFA (PIV) for admin roles; RBAC; quarterly access recertifications [RFP pp. 36, 45–46, 55, 99].                                                                                    ┃

┃ C. Accessibility (Section 508) Package                                                                                                                                                     ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  1 DoD-style Documentation of Conformance (DoD) snippet (for proposal insertion) As required by RFP pp. 22–24, our solution conforms to Section 508 using DHS OAST Trusted Tester and WCAG ┃
┃    2.2 AA. Definition of Done includes: (1) zero open High/Medium Trusted Tester findings; (2) successful WCAG 2.2 AA tests or approved equivalent facilitation; (3) validated artifacts   ┃
┃    (TT logs, contrast checks, SR transcripts, PAC PDF reports); (4) accurate captions and audio description for training media; (5) approved VPAT/ACR (VPAT 2.5) with evidence links; (6)  ┃
┃    PM and Accessibility Lead sign-off prior to release. Accessibility remains in CI/CD via automated checks plus manual audits for complex interactions.                                   ┃
┃  2 Checklist (condensed)                                                                                                                                                                   ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • Keyboard operability, no traps; visible focus [2.1.1, 2.1.2, 2.4.11/13] – QA Lead                                                                                                       ┃
┃  • Contrast (text/UI) [1.4.3, 1.4.11]; reflow/text spacing [1.4.10/12] – QA Lead                                                                                                           ┃
┃  • Non-text content, use of color [1.1.1, 1.4.1] – Accessibility Lead                                                                                                                      ┃
┃  • Structure/semantics [1.3.1/1.3.2], bypass blocks [2.4.1] – Accessibility Lead                                                                                                           ┃
┃  • Link purpose, label in name [2.4.4, 2.5.3] – QA/Accessibility                                                                                                                           ┃
┃  • Errors/status messages [3.3.x, 4.1.2/4.1.3] – QA/Accessibility                                                                                                                          ┃
┃  • Target size, dragging alternatives [2.5.8, 2.5.7] – QA                                                                                                                                  ┃
┃  • Timing/pause controls [2.2.1/2.2.2] – QA                                                                                                                                                ┃
┃  • Documentation/training media (PDF/UA, captions, audio description) – Accessibility/QA                                                                                                   ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  3 RACI                                                                                                                                                                                    ┃
┃                                                                                                                                                                                            ┃
┃  • Plan: PM (A), Accessibility Lead (R), QA Lead (C), Dev Lead (C)                                                                                                                         ┃
┃  • Implement: Dev Lead (R), Accessibility (C), QA (C), PM (I)                                                                                                                              ┃
┃  • Test (TT): QA (R), Accessibility (C), Dev (I), PM (I)                                                                                                                                   ┃
